***granola.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a> (69786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Genericization of <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Granola" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Granola"><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>Granola</a></a></i>, name of an early <a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>brand</a> of the cereal, itself a variation of <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Granula" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Granula">Granula</a></i>, invented by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Caleb_Jackson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:James Caleb Jackson">James Caleb Jackson</a> in 1863. <i>Granula</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> named after the <span class="Latn" lang="en">granules</span> of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Graham_flour" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Graham flour">Graham flour</a>, the main ingredient<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">granolas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A breakfast and snack food consisting of loose, <a href = vnd.unilang:crispy.html>crispy</a> pellets made of <a href = vnd.unilang:nuts.html>nuts</a>, rolled oats, honey and other natural ingredients.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:crunchy.html>crunchy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">granola-head</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly Canada, US<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of a person</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Eating healthy food, supporting the protection of the environment, and having liberal views.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">You see more and more of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hippie.html>hippie</a> activist <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a> these days.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b> November 21,  <a href = vnd.unilang:jame.html>Jame</a> Schaefer |  Tobias Winright,  <cite>Environmental Justice and Climate Change</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=zG1BAgAAQBAJ">[2]</a></sup>, page 228:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>behind them a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></b>-looking mom in denim <a href = vnd.unilang:overalls.html>overalls</a> and a t-shirt <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> pulling in to do her drop-off . . . from a <a href = vnd.unilang:prius.html>Prius</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2015</b> February 13,  Dennis Saffran,  “<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://thefederalist.com/2015/02/13/the-orwellian-campaign-to-project-anti-vaccination-onto-republicans/">The Orwellian Campaign To Project Anti-Vaccination Onto Republicans</a>”, in  <cite>The Federalist</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Rather, the anti-vax movement <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> almost entirely a phenomenon of the affluent <a href = vnd.unilang:crunchy.html>crunchy</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></b> Left—as everyone across the political spectrum acknowledged until the last week or so.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2020</b> June 18,  Kiera <a href = vnd.unilang:butler.html>Butler</a>,  “<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.motherjones.com/politics/2020/06/the-anti-vax-movements-radical-shift-from-crunchy-granola-purists-to-far-right-crusaders/">The Anti-Vax Movement’s Radical Shift From <a href = vnd.unilang:crunchy.html>Crunchy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>Granola</a> Purists to Far-Right Crusaders</a>”, in  <cite>Mother Jones</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Yet some <a href = vnd.unilang:experts.html>experts</a> believe that <a href = vnd.unilang:voices.html>voices</a> from the far right are beginning to drown out those of the <a href = vnd.unilang:crunchy.html>crunchy</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></b> crowd.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***grapefruit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grapefruit.html>grapefruit</a> (21348)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grapefruit.html>grapefruit</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***grappa.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grappa.html>grappa</a> (42223)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:grappa.html>grappa</a></i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grape</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grappa.html>grappa</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">grappas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An Italian grape-based spirit of between 80 and 100 proof, made from the distillation of pomace.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A variety or serving of <a href = vnd.unilang:grappa.html>grappa</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b> February 14,  Florence Fabricant,  “Off the Menu”, in  <cite>New York Times</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2007/02/14/dining/14off.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Wines, a few <a href = vnd.unilang:cocktails.html>cocktails</a> and <b>grappas</b> but no mixed drinks: 34 Downing Street (Bedford Street)</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:drinken.html>drinken</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> Italiaanse <a href = vnd.unilang:alcoholisch.html>alcoholische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drank.html>drank</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vervaardigd.html>vervaardigd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> destillatie <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:restanten.html>restanten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:druiven.html>druiven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> wijnbereiding</li></ol>

***grasshopper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grasshopper.html>grasshopper</a> (69784)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">gressehopper</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:grashopper.html>grashopper</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">grashoppyr</i>, alteration of earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">grashope</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">grashoppe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">greshoppe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">græshoppa</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">gærshoppa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:grasshopper.html>grasshopper</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grass</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a></i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Gäärshupper</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">grashupper</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">grashipper</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Grashüpper</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Gresshüpper</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Grashüpfer</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">græshoppe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">gräshoppa</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">gresshoppe</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grasshopper.html>grasshopper</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">grasshoppers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A herbivorous insect of the order Orthoptera, noted for its ability to jump long <a href = vnd.unilang:distances.html>distances</a> and for the habit of some species communicating by stridulation; they are related to but distinct from <a href = vnd.unilang:crickets.html>crickets</a>.
<ol><li>In the strict sense, refers to insects in the suborder Caelifera, particularly those in the family Acrididae.</li>
<li>In a <a href = vnd.unilang:looser.html>looser</a> sense, also includes the katydids (also known as longhorned grasshoppers or bush <a href = vnd.unilang:crickets.html>crickets</a>), which are members of the family Tettigoniidae, of the suborder Ensifera.</li></ol>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">grasshop</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms hyponym"><span class="defdate">Hyponym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">locust</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A cocktail made with crème <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:menthe.html>menthe</a> and optionally with crème <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cacao.html>cacao</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A young student in initial <a href = vnd.unilang:stages.html>stages</a> of training who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> chosen on account of their obvious <a href = vnd.unilang:talent.html>talent</a>.
<ul><li><b>2009</b>, B.P. Terpstra, <i>Quadrant</i>, November 2009, No. 461 (Volume LIII, Number 11), Quadrant Magazine Limited, page 2:
<dl><dd>Although <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> know exactly <i>why</i> Li <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> chosen to dance, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> witness a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> assuring <a href = vnd.unilang:officials.html>officials</a> that the child isn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> from bourgeois stock. Phew. There are no known landowners in the family, so the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grasshopper.html>grasshopper</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:passes.html>passes</a> some cultural purity test, in a state often fixated on class warfare, driven by the cult of personality, and bullied by <a href = vnd.unilang:paranoia.html>paranoia</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> In ordinary square or upright pianos of London make, the escapement <a href = vnd.unilang:lever.html>lever</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a>, so made that it can be <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> out and replaced with the key.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hopper.html>hopper</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Grove to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grasshopper.html>grasshopper</a> engine</span></li>
<li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/grasshopper_lobster" class="extiw" title="w:grasshopper lobster"><a href = vnd.unilang:grasshopper.html>grasshopper</a> lobster</a></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grasshopper.html>grasshopper</a> warbler</span></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:grau.html>grau</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*grāo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grēwaz</i>.

<dl><dd><i>In Victorian slums grey <a href = vnd.unilang:rags.html>rags</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ware.html>ware</a> indicative of grim poverty, in a modern favella one <a href = vnd.unilang:sees.html>sees</a> mostly bright colors</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

Ykema, 13.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tweede.html>tweede</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:derde.html>derde</a> maendt <a href = vnd.unilang:sal.html>sal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> haer <a href = vnd.unilang:bien.html>bien</a></dd>
<dd>Sachte handtplackens <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:propere.html>propere</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grauwen.html>grauwen</a></b>,
<dl><dd>The second and third month one should offer them</dd>
<dd>moderate application of the paddle and appropriate <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snaps.html>snaps</a></b>,</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:graveren.html>graveren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:graver.html>graver</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*graban</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grabaną</i>. ***greep.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:greep.html>greep</a> (3389)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijpen.html>grepe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gripi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grasp, clutch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gripiz</i>. A variant nominative singular form, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> preserved in <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begrip.html>begrip</a></i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>grasp, clutches

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijpen.html>grepe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*grēpa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">handle, <a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*graipō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:greep.html>greep</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grepen.html>grepen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:greep.html>greepje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a>, handle
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:handvat.html>handvat</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:greep.html>greep</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention"> singular past indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijpen.html>grijpen</a></i></span></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>In the sense of random guess, only the example provided <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> common usage. For example, while you can say <i><a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>Doe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gok.html>gok</a></i> or <i><a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>Doe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gooi.html>gooi</a></i> (take a guess), you can'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> say <i><a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>Doe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greep.html>greep</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***grein.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grein.html>grein</a> (129989)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:grein.html>grein</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">grain</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">grānum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵr̥h₂nóm</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublette with Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:graan.html>graan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which descended directly from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">grānum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grein.html>grein</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grein.html>greinen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grein.html>greintje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a small something; a grain</li></ol>

***grens.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grens.html>grens</a> (1693)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed in the 16th century from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">grense</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">grenitse</i> and/or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:grenzen.html>Grenze</a></i>, both ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Polish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Polish">Old Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="zlw-opl">granica</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*granica</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grens.html>grens</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grenzen.html>grenzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grens.html>grensje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>border, frontier</li>
<li>limit</li></ol>

***gribus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gribus.html>gribus</a> (57343)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gribus.html>gribus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gribus.html>gribussen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gribus.html>gribusje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">prison</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">clink</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">slammer</span>
<ul><li><b>1854</b>, A. Nauta, <i>Emilia <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Nassau, <a href = vnd.unilang:prinses.html>prinses</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Portugal. <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:historisch.html>historisch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:romantisch.html>romantisch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verhaal.html>verhaal</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gebroeders.html>Gebroeders</a> Diederichs (publ.), 195.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwam.html>kwam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> voorspraak <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stade.html>stade</a>: want <a href = vnd.unilang:zonder.html>zonder</a> dezelve <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeker.html>zeker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:reeds.html>reeds</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geknipt.html>geknipt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geworden.html>geworden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gribus.html>gribus</a></b> – zoo <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevangenis.html>gevangenis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noemde.html>noemde</a> – teregt <a href = vnd.unilang:gekomen.html>gekomen</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1901</b>, Justus <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Maurik, "<a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>Te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergunning.html>vergunning</a>. Amsterdamsche <a href = vnd.unilang:schets.html>Schets</a>.", in <i>Burgerluidjes. Volksuitgave</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> Holkema amp; Warendorf (1901, 8th edition, 1st edition from 1884), 74.</li>
<li>‘(...) <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> in den <a href = vnd.unilang:gribus.html>Gribus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:misschien.html>misschien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>morgen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a>. (...)’
<dl><dd><dl><dd>‘If he <a href = vnd.unilang:ends.html>ends</a> up in the <b>clink</b>, they might also keep him there tomorrow.’</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a> (64891)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Origin uncertain, perhaps related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">griddle</i>.  The ending <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> assimilated to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">iron</i>. <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(<span id="rfv-etymology-notice-en-"></span>Can this<sup class="plainlinks">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/w/index.php?title=Wiktionary:Etymology_scriptorium/2020/Augustamp;action=editamp;section=newamp;preload=Template:rfv-etymology/preloadamp;preloadtitle=%5B%5Bgridiron%23rfv-etymology-notice-en-%7cgridiron%5D%5D">+</a>)</sup> etymology be sourced?)</span>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Nyam%21.jpg/220px-Nyam%21.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Nyam%21.jpg/330px-Nyam%21.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Nyam%21.jpg/440px-Nyam%21.jpg 2x" data-file-width="700" data-file-height="525" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A <a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a></div></div></div>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gridirons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An instrument of torture on which people <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> secured before being burned by fire. <span class="defdate">[from 13th c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1603</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michel_de_Montaigne" class="extiw" title="w:Michel de Montaigne"><a href = vnd.unilang:michel.html>Michel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:montaigne.html>Montaigne</a></a>,  chapter 32, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Florio" class="extiw" title="w:John Florio">John Florio</a>, transl., <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Essays_(Montaigne)" class="extiw" title="w:Essays (Montaigne)">The Essayes,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="or, Morall, Politike and Millitarie Discourses of Lo. Michaell de Montaigne, Knight of the Noble Order of St. Michaell, and One of the Gentlemen in Ordinary of the French King, Henry the Third His Chamber">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite>, book II, printed at London |  By <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Valentine_Simmes" class="extiw" title="w:Valentine Simmes"><a href = vnd.unilang:val.html>Val</a>[entine] Simmes</a> for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Edward Blount</a><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="dwelling in Paules churchyard">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/946730821">946730821</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I know, there have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> found seely boores, who have rather endure to have their <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a> broiled upon a <b>Greedyron</b>, their <a href = vnd.unilang:fingers.html>fingers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ends.html>ends</a> crusht and wrung with the lock of a Pistoll, their <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> all bloody to be thrust out of their heads with wringing and wresting of a cord about their foreheads, before they would so much as be ransomed.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>An iron rack or grate used for broiling meat and fish <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> coals. <span class="defdate">[from 14th c.]</span></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From resembling the shape of a <a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a> (a square rectilinear grid)
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gridirons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any object resembling the rack or grate. <span class="defdate">[from 15th c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b>,  Andrew Martin,  <cite>Underground Overground: A passenger's history of the Tube</cite>, Profile Books, →ISBN, page 55:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Just north of Farringdon station, and to the east of <a href = vnd.unilang:ray.html>Ray</a> Street, there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a wide cutting bounded by another of those brick walls nicely calculated to be just too high for you to see <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>. So prop your bike against it, and stand on the down-pointing pedal crank. You are <a href = vnd.unilang:looking.html>looking</a> at the <a href = vnd.unilang:ray.html>Ray</a> Street <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>Gridiron</a></b>, a spectacular bridge in a cutting that <a href = vnd.unilang:carries.html>carries</a> the Metropolitan, the supposed Underground, <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the Widened Lines (now Thameslink).</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An openwork frame on which vessels are placed for examination, cleaning, and repairs.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A raised framework from which lighting <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> suspended.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">American football</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The field on which American football <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> played. <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand" class="extiw" title="w:New Zealand">New Zealand</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> American and Canadian football, particularly when used to distinguish from other <a href = vnd.unilang:codes.html>codes</a> of football.
<ul><li><b>1995</b> October 3, <a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a> O′Shea, <i>Sports: Out on the field</i>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Advocate" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Advocate">The Advocate</a></i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=2WQEAAAAMBAJamp;pg=PA54amp;dq=%22gridiron+player%22%7C%22gridiron+players%22+-intitle:%22%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=XuhuT5_QCNGImQXR25iVBgamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22gridiron%20player%22%7C%22gridiron%20players%22%20-intitle%3A%22%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">page 54</a>,
<dl><dd>He represented Australia in this year′s rugby tour of England and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> as well-known in Australia as any top <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a></b> player <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in the United States.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2001</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Langston_Hughes" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Langston Hughes">Langston Hughes</a>, Dolan Hubbard, <i>Jackie Robinson: First Negro in Big League Baseball: 1919—</i>, <i>The Collected Works of Langston Hughes, Volume 12: Works for Children and Young Adults</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=LLhfJ5rlgKECamp;pg=PA105amp;dq=%22gridiron+player%22%7C%22gridiron+players%22+-intitle:%22%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=XuhuT5_QCNGImQXR25iVBgamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22gridiron%20player%22%7C%22gridiron%20players%22%20-intitle%3A%22%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">page 106</a>,
<dl><dd>So Jackie′s name became known far and wide as an exceptional <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a></b> player.</dd></dl></li>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gridiron.html>gridiron</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">gridirons</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">gridironing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">gridironed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To mark or cover with lines; to crisscross.
<ul><li><b>1901</b>, Archibald John Little, <i>Mount <a href = vnd.unilang:omi.html>Omi</a> and Beyond: A Record of Travel on the Thibetan Border</i>, Cambridge University Press, 2010, Conclusion, p. 242, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=4VxiopcUE6sCamp;printsec=frontcoverv=onepageamp;qamp;f=false">[1]</a>
<dl><dd>This basin of Szechuan (literally "Four <a href = vnd.unilang:streams.html>Streams</a>," but which, reading the character idiographically, I should be inclined to render as "<b>Gridironed</b> by <a href = vnd.unilang:streams.html>Streams</a>"), <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1923</b>, Maximilian P.E. Groszmann, <i>A Parent's Manual: Child Problems, Mental and Moral</i>, New York: Century, p. 74, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=HzhJAAAAIAAJamp;q=%22gridironing%22amp;dq=%22gridironing%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ved=0ahUKEwjmg834ypPNAhUT3GMKHTdHAqYQ6AEI4gEwKA">[2]</a>
<dl><dd>Another logical method <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that of <b>gridironing</b> the field by a series of straight paths that are parallel to each other.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1924</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herman_Melville" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Herman Melville">Herman Melville</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Billy_Budd" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Billy Budd"><a href = vnd.unilang:billy.html>Billy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:budd.html>Budd</a></a></i>, London: Constable amp; Co., Chapter 8, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://gutenberg.net.au/ebooks06/0608511h.html">[3]</a>
<dl><dd>When <a href = vnd.unilang:billy.html>Billy</a> saw the culprit's naked back under the scourge <b>gridironed</b> with red welts, and worse <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <a href = vnd.unilang:billy.html>Billy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> horrified.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1949</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lewis_Sinclair" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lewis Sinclair"><a href = vnd.unilang:lewis.html>Lewis</a> Sinclair</a>, <i>The God-Seeker</i>, New York: Popular Library, Chapter 42, p. 227,
<dl><dd>His white back, <b>gridironed</b> with scars, <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> as soft as a <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a>'s.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2012</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:janet.html>Janet</a> Wallach, <i>The Richest Woman in America: Hetty Green in the Gilded Age</i>, New York: Anchor Books, 2013, Chapter 8, p. 111, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=oKvaLKx8rEgCamp;printsec=frontcoverv=onepageamp;qamp;f=false">[4]</a>
<dl><dd>Railways spanned the continent and <b>gridironed</b> the states.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand" class="extiw" title="w:New Zealand">New Zealand</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To purchase <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> so that the remaining adjacent sections are <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a> than the minimum area purchasable as freehold, thus excluding potential freeholders.</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">grippe</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">gripper</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to seize, snatch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*grīpan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grīpaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰreyb-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grab, grasp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijpen.html>grijpen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Grippe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flu</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grippe</i>.

***griet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:griet.html>griet</a> (3797)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>An onomatopoeia.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:griet.html>griet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grieten.html>grieten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grietje.html>grietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>alternative form of grutto (the bird godwit)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the Dutch girl's name <a href = vnd.unilang:margriet.html>Margriet</a>, cognate with English Margaret.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:griet.html>griet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grieten.html>grieten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grietje.html>grietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> girl, (young or any) female, often derogatory: broad</li></ol>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:griet.html>griet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grieten.html>grieten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grietje.html>grietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>short for <a href = vnd.unilang:margriet.html>margriet</a>, an apple variety</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grietje.html>grietje</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>An euphemistic alteration of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in curse <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>, to remove the blasphemous nature.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:griet.html>griet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>euphemism for <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>, notable as an alternative for blasphemous cursing</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***grievous.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grievous.html>grievous</a> (42219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grieven.html>grieve</a></i>, from the <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">greven</i>, from the <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">grever</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gravō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I burden</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Developed in the 13th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grievous.html>grievous</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:grievous.html>grievous</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:grievous.html>grievous</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Causing grief, pain or sorrow.
<ul><li><b>1883</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Louis_Stevenson" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Louis Stevenson">Robert <a href = vnd.unilang:louis.html>Louis</a> Stevenson</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Treasure_Island" class="extiw" title="w:Treasure Island">Treasure Island</a></i>
<dl><dd>As for the <a href = vnd.unilang:captain.html>captain</a>, his wounds <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grievous.html>grievous</a></b> indeed but not dangerous.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Serious, grave, dire or dangerous.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>See also Thesaurus:lamentable</li></ul>
</body>

***griffin.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:griffin.html>griffin</a> (6818)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">griffoun</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">griffon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gryphus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γρύψ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grúps</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Cotta_Greif_1839.jpg/220px-Cotta_Greif_1839.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="241" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Cotta_Greif_1839.jpg/330px-Cotta_Greif_1839.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Cotta_Greif_1839.jpg/440px-Cotta_Greif_1839.jpg 2x" data-file-width="726" data-file-height="794" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>a <a href = vnd.unilang:griffin.html>griffin</a> (1)</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:griffin.html>griffin</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:griffins.html>griffins</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A mythical beast having the body of a lion and the wings and head of an eagle.</li>
<li>A large vulture (<i>Gyps fulvus</i>) found in the mountainous parts of Southern Europe, North Africa, and Asia Minor, supposed to be the "eagle" of the Bible.</li>
<li>An English variety of apple.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/India" class="extiw" title="w:India">India</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> just arrived from Europe.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1842</b>,  <cite>The Asiatic journal and monthly register</cite>, volume 38, page 40:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Tables <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> laid out in the palace, profusely covered with wines and refreshments, in the European style; old hands and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:griffins.html>griffins</a></b>, fair sex and civilians, seemed all determined to enjoy themselves<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of H. Kingsley to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A cadet newly arrived in British India: <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> English, <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> Indian.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup></li>
<li>A watchful guardian, especially a duenna in charge of a young woman.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/bearded_griffin" class="extiw" title="w:bearded griffin">bearded <a href = vnd.unilang:griffin.html>griffin</a></a> (<i>Gypaetus barbatus</i>)</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">griffinish</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">griffinism</span></li></ul>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gripen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">grīpan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grīpaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰreyb-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grasp, grab</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***grijs.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grijs.html>grijs</a> (5335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijs.html>grijs</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*grīs</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grīsaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijs.html>grijs</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijzer.html>grijzer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grijs.html>grijs</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">grijst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">grey</span>, grey-colored</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> referring to grey hair</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">old</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">weathered</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">tarnished</span>, affected by wear and tear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gozer.html>Gozer</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> ille <a href = vnd.unilang:plaat.html>plaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jantje.html>Jantje</a> Smitje <a href = vnd.unilang:helemaal.html>helemaal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grijs.html>grijs</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedraaid.html>gedraaid</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Dude, I wore that wicked record by <a href = vnd.unilang:jantje.html>Jantje</a> Smitje completely out.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>partially illegal</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijs.html>grijs</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijs.html>grijzen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>the color grey, any mix of black and white</li></ol>

***gril.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gril.html>gril</a> (20788)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">grille</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cricket</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Grille</i>).  Perhaps the shift in sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to a conflation of <a href = vnd.unilang:crickets.html>crickets</a> with earwigs, involving the popular myth of insects which crawl through the ears to lay eggs in the brain, altering a person's behaviour.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gril.html>gril</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grillen.html>grillen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gril.html>grilletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:caprice.html>caprice</a>, whim, impulse</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
